<U>Messages<UC><C><L.36.1>

<Z>Christmas Post <C> The ritual warning that as Christmas approaches, the post will grind to a halt. Given it already has,<L.31.1>
backwards may be the next step, so don't be surprised if the postmen start calling to return post they've already delivered!!!!<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>9am Deadline <C> Can I remind everyone that orders should be here by 9am (which for postal users means the previous day's<L.31.1>
post). A few people seem to be dribbling in email orders during the morning (or afternoon) so be warned, they will miss the boat.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Gameplan Baseball <C> The newsletter with a host of discussion points and possible developments for Gameplan Baseball is still<L.31.1>
available, and I'm keen for comments. Those of you playing by post should have had a copy, those by email can download it from<L.31.1>
www.pbmsports.com via the Rules and Newsletters link. Comments are more than welcome. There's a whole host of possibilities, and<L.31.1>
I'm not suggesting all of them will come in now, or indeed at all, but feedback on any or all is welcome.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Late Email Results <C> If you think results are late, please make sure you wait until the following morning before chasing up<L.31.1>
results. First step is to check out the Latest News at www.pbmsports.com - if I am running late I'll post a notice there. Please<L.31.1>
don't chase me up because you know your mate got his half an hour ago, because whilst most emails are "instant", often they do get<L.31.1>
delayed for a few hours and it does take a while to send them all out (I spread them out to avoid triggering firewalls).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
Equally however, if it's the next morning and you've not had results, and there's nothing on www.pbmsports.com saying I've had a<L.31.1>
problem, then please chase me up. If it hasn't shown 12 hours later, odds are it won't, and probably some firewall or spam filter<L.31.1>
somewhere has gobbled it (and they do appear to do so without pattern). I'd rather you ended up with two copies than none.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>PDF Reports <C> Emailed game reports are available for all games here. The standard format is a PDF file - Adobe Reader is free<L.31.1>
to download (see www.pbmsports.com for a link) and you can open your reports with one click of the mouse and you can either view<L.31.1>
them on screen, or print them as you wish. You don't need to worry about formatting or printer drivers. The text format for<L.31.1>
reports is available but I only expect people will want to do so if they use the text file for other purposes (such as exporting<L.31.1>
the listings into software produced yourself). If you've not tried email reports before, try them out - it really is very easy.  <L.31.1>
